<td style="font-size: larger;">7
</td>
<td>Stamps Books tell YOUR story. Inside you'll find all the pins you've found, the games you've mastered, and the medals you've earned. Customize yours to show others what you like... and what you can do!
</td></tr>

<td style="font-size: larger;">7
</td>
<td>Ninjas must give their all facing one another in battle. Though matches are fierce, Sensei teaches that competition is the best way to improve your skill. Win or lose, ninjas always remain loyal allies, so remember to tell your opponent "good game!"
</td></tr>

<td style="font-size: larger;">7
</td>
<td>Each part of the Water Ninja Suit is a symbol of skill. They must be earned in order – first the <a href="/wiki/Wave_Sandals" title="Wave Sandals">Water Sandals</a>, then the <a href="/wiki/Waterfall_Coat" title="Waterfall Coat">Waterfall Coat</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Torrent_Mask" title="Torrent Mask">Torrent Mask</a>. Once you earn the <a href="/wiki/Helmet_of_Oceans" title="Helmet of Oceans">Helmet of Oceans</a>, you're ready to face Sensei.
</td></tr>

<td style="font-size: larger;">7
</td>
<td>The rainstorm in November 2010 was a sign that ninjas were ready to master the element of water. Sensei soon announced the construction of the Water Dojo. It opened on November 25... and Card-Jitsu Water training began.
</td></tr>
